[30;1m49 | [0m[35m**Maintenance cost, code cleanup**[0m
[30;1m50 | [0m[35m  `OpenERP` has evolved a lot since the version 5.0 (2009), making `OERPLib`[0m
[30;1m51 | [0m[35m  hard to maintain (write tests for all versions before each `OERPLib` and[0m
[30;1m52 | [0m[35m  `OpenERP` release is very time consuming). All the compatibility code for[0m
[30;1m53 | [0m[35m  `OpenERP` 5.0 to 7.0 was dropped for `OdooRPC`, making the project more[0m
[30;1m54 | [0m[35m  maintainable. `Odoo` is now a more mature product, and `OdooRPC` should[0m
[30;1m55 | [0m[35m  suffer less about compatibility issues from one release to another.[0m
